<Pics>None< /Pics>< review>
01/27/2021

** BEWARE -- This is not a place to take your vehicle, shady stuff going on. **

I had a groupon for a 4 wheel alignment. I called them yesterday and they stated to come in today at 2PM. When I got there, I was informed the internet was down and they could not complete the alignment. I have the ability to work remotely so I let them know i'll work from their lobby and if the internet comes up that is good, but if not, i'll return another day.

Towards the end of the day at 4:45PM, the technician comes back into the lobby and states the internet did not come back up and will have to try another day. I was ok with this as i took the chance of it not coming back up.

When I asked for my keys, the technician went into the garage to retrieve them and then told me that my front two windows are completely down and that it just started raining. I told him i NEVER leave my windows down especially on a rainy day. He then said... I'm just letting know as to imply that i left my windows down. The car was completely drenched on the inside. In addition, my two hubcaps on the passenger were not completely secured and they were just hanging on there partially secured.

I can't help but wonder 1) why did they put both windows down, 2) what work did they really do by taking the two hubcaps off and 3) there was no work authorization form completed? If their internet was down, there was no reason for them to even get in my vehicle....

I cancelled the groupon and will be taking my business elsewhere. I've always been the type of person to support local business, unfortunately this is not one of them.

** BEWARE -- This is not a place to take your vehicle, shady stuff going on. **</review>

We go to this place every time we visit Tahoe. They have a variety of flavored Olive oils and balsamic vinegars, all high quality. < review>
Park Fly & Save is a good budget option for parking at the airport. Find their website and book in advance, putting down a deposit. With taxes and fees it came out to just about $10/ day. (The advertised $5.95 I first saw was without those.)

I had to wait for about 10 minutes for a shuttle to pick me up, but it dropped me off right at the terminal. When I returned to the airport and needed the shuttle, I just missed one and had to wait about 15 minutes for the shuttle to come around again. (I believe this lot has just one.) As everyone had been waiting for 15 minutes, the shuttle was extremely full, to the point where half the riders were standing for the trip back to the lot.

When we arrived to the lot, I disembarked, found my car, drove to the exit, and paid the remainder of my balance. However, the majority of the people from my shuttle were standing around waiting. They had evidently taken a different reservation approach and their cars were valet parked, meaning they had to continue waiting for their cars to be brought out. My advice: Don't go for that option.

Overall, a convenient enough parking option at a rate much lower than on airport parking.<//review>

<user_name>Meredith Hand< /user_name><Date>1456883932586<//Date><rating>4< /rating>< Text>
Longer review fell into the deepest depths of the interwebs. Cuisine remind me a lot of my favorite place from my college years in Davis-- so disappointed when they changed ownership. My go-tos of bhaigan bharta and chicken tika marsala were delicious, my husband inhaled my leftovers when I got home. Mango lassi was a mango lassi, hard to get it wrong-- yum.

Four stars because our entrees came out thirty minutes after the soup and salad ordered by those in our party who wanted lighter fare. They were likely bringing out the appetizer-type orders first, common enough mistake, but we'd made it clear we weren't really sharing. They also forgot a member of our party's coffee, and she thought it tasted/smelled horrible when it came; the water in our glasses was the same and it tasted fine... and I'm picky as hell about that. They did give us separate checks, though this probably added to the confusion, but still-- it shouldn't be too hard to handle a four-top at noon with the restaurant at only half-capacity.

The waiters and bussers were hotttt. *cough*

I'll up it to five if the service is better next time.<//Text>

The good: the wait staff were friendly and accommodating. The atmosphere was warm and inviting. They gave my sister a free drink for her birthday.

The ok: the food. Not bad, but nothing to write home about. The tortillas are pretty good.
